1. We are staying with our baby. Considering the baby's feeding problem, we specially chose a hotel that can deliver meals to the room. When checking in, we also specifically asked the front desk staff if we could order food to be delivered to the room, and they told us that it was completely possible. After checking in, I took my children to the restaurant on the second floor to order food. I was told that we would not be able to order food in the next few days. The reason was that there were many wedding banquets and the chef did not have time to cook for us! ! ! ! Let's order takeout! ! ! If it can't be done, why use this as a gimmick to promote it? ? ? When we left the hotel, we happened to meet a young couple checking in with their baby, and the front desk introduced that meals could be delivered to the room! So funny~~This is the service of a so-called five-star hotel? Nonsense!
2. Take the baby back to the hotel for a nap in the afternoon. At about three o'clock, the cleaning lady knocked on the door and rang the doorbell. We got up quickly and went to the door to tell the aunt that there was no need to clean. Who knows in a few seconds, the aunt opened the door and pushed in. Because of the hotel room type, you can see the bed when you open the door. My partner had just finished taking a shower and before he had time to get dressed, his aunt pushed the door open and saw him. No privacy at all! ! ! ! ! ! If it weren't for the fact that the child was asleep and I didn't want to make any noise, I would really want to explode the quintessence of Chinese culture! ! ! ! ! It only takes a few seconds for the aunt to go from knocking on the door to taking the key card to open the door. Don’t you have any quality? I wonder if there is anyone in the room first? ? ? ? Just ask who dares to stay in this kind of hotel with peace of mind? ? ? ?
3. There were insects crawling around in the breakfast dining area. I stayed in a big hotel because I wanted to be hygienic, but I didn't expect that there were bugs roaming around in the dining area, which shows the health and safety issues. Why didn't I take pictures of the bugs? Because the first time I saw a bug was to pick up the baby and keep the baby away from the bugs wandering on the ground.
4. The sound insulation is very poor. The person next door spoke clearly.
The negative review is given, no matter how the hotel responds, I just want to say that it is fair and reasonable, and I only told my true experience!

msg:經常住酒店很少寫點評，這家酒店挺令人印象深刻的。這次早到，延遲，忘東西一大堆事情都遇上了，每一件事處理的都很好，彬彬有禮而且有效迅速。這個太重要了，直接把酒店印象分推到高位。單説忘東西在房間裏這事，衹有這家酒店主動打電話詢問。之前有幾次住在國際大牌酒店裡忘拿東西了，不論是住的套房還是我本人是高級會員，這些酒店都沒有主動通知我忘拿東西，事後想起來打電話去詢問也是回覆很慢。體驗很差。
最後感謝酒店人美心善的小姐姐Jennifer，還有一樓那麼冷還每次都堅持打招呼的接待們，一切都很好很温馨。期待有機會再次入住。

msg:因為假期堵車隨手看了一眼攜程，訂到了甩賣特價房，事實證明平台總有驚喜在等你。特價房高級雙床房，我們一家三口拼一下床，睡得好舒服，床墊和枕頭的比例很和諧。冰箱裏還有免費小飲料喝，非常感謝🙏，開了一天車、真的需要一口可樂。
早飯中規中矩，意外好吃的是水果、茶葉蛋和小肉包～
走了還丟了東西在酒店，居然還按照原價賠償了，服務態度是好的有點過分了……真的不太好意思。感謝酒店讓我們旅途中有個舒服的歇腳之地。

msg:房間一般般，付費460.8元。
差評就兩個原因:1 説好的水果送，我等了十幾分鍾，沒人送，打電話給前台，前台支支吾吾等了半天，也沒反饋。
2.我凌晨2點多才到，特別困，一天的大霧天開車很累，睡到第二天下午1:20剛起來洗漱，1:30在上廁所接到電話:1:30了，退房。我説你們網上明明標註麼得2:00，對方是個女的，説“哦，2點吧”，服務非常隨意，趕人走。我交了300的按金是***？
你如果是100塊錢的房間，我也就不要求你什麼了，我花了460塊錢就為了聽前台來*我。這種酒店我整個鹽城住了那麼多萬豪。還有希爾頓，我從來沒有看過其他的房間。像你們這麼樣的差的服務態度。不推薦任何人來，如果想被*的話繼續來吧。距離位置本來就是靠在高速邊上，有點偏遠。港府的洲際酒店還有其他的酒店我也住過，這是我所有鹽城第一市住的服務態度非常的惡劣，非常隨意的一家酒店。
港府大飯店，想被*你就來。
